dependencyGraphBuilder,\n    55→// which builds a graph caching the dependencies among objects. Triggered by the\n    56→// graph changes, the dependencyGraphBuilder enqueues objects that can\n    57→// potentially be garbage-collected to the `attemptToDelete` queue, and enqueues\n    58→// objects whose dependents need to be orphaned to the `attemptToOrphan` queue.\n    59→// The GarbageCollector has workers who consume these two queues, send requests\n    60→// to the API server to delete/update the objects accordingly.\n    61→// Note that having the dependencyGraphBuilder notify the garbage collector\n    62→// ensures that the garbage collector operates with a graph that is at least as\n    63→// up to date as the notification is sent.\n    64→type GarbageCollector struct {\n    65→\trestMapper     meta.ResettableRESTMapper\n    66→\tmetadataClient metadata.Interface\n  clientset.Interface\n    76→\teventBroadcaster record.EventBroadcaster\n    77→}\n    78→\n    79→var _ controller.Interface = (*GarbageCollector)(nil)\n    80→var _ controller.Debuggable = KUBERNETES/KUBERNETES\n\n### Signal Handler Registration\n- **staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/signal.go** (abstraction)\n  - Functions: `SetupSignalHandler()`, `SetupSignalContext()`\n  - Pattern: Creates a signal handler for SIGTERM and SIGINT\n  - Shutdown on first signal, exit on second signal\n  - Returns context that can be cancelled\n\n- **staging/src/k8s.io/sample-controller/pkg/signals/signal.go** (reference implementation)\n  - Functions: `SetupSignalHandler()`\n  - Pattern: Similar to apiserver implementation\n  - Platform-specific: signal_posix.go, signal_windows.go\n\n- **pkg/util/interrupt/interrupt.go** (utility handler)\n  - Type: `Handler` with methods `Run()`, `Signal()`, `Close()`\n  - Pattern: Wraps signal.Notify with guaranteed cleanup\n  - Uses sync.Once for single execution guarantee\n  - Defers cleanup operations\n\n### Signal Handler Usage\n- **cmd/kube-apiserver/app/server.go**\n  - Uses: `genericapiserver.SetupSignalContext()`\n  - Pattern: Context passed through cobra command\n\n- **cmd/kube-scheduler/app/server.go**\n  - Uses: SetupSignalContext pattern\n  \n- **cmd/kubelet/app/server.go**\n  - Uses: Signal handling for graceful shutdown\n\n### Controller Shutdown Patterns\n- **pkg/controller/garbagecollector/garbagecollector.go**\n  - Type: `GarbageCollector` controller\n  - Pattern: Context-based cancellation propagation\n  - Work queue management with graceful draining\n\n- **pkg/controller/resourcequota/resource_quota_controller.go**\n  - Pattern: Context-based shutdown\n\n- **pkg/controller/storageversionmigrator/storageversionmigrator.go**\n  - Pattern: Migration controller with graceful stop\n\n### Direct Signal Handling\n- **staging/src/k8s.io/client-go/example_test.go**\n  - Pattern: Direct signal.Notify(sigCh, syscall.SIGINT, syscall.SIGTERM)\n\n- **staging/src/k8s.io/client-go/examples/leader-election/main.go**\n  - Pattern: Leader election with signal handling\n  - Usage: signal.Notify(ch, os.Interrupt, syscall.SIGTERM)\n\n- **staging/src/k8s.io/kms/internal/plugins/_mock/plugin.go**\n  - Pattern: Mock plugin with signal handling\n\n---\n\n## 2. GRAFANA/GRAFANA\n\n### Main Server Initialization and Shutdown\n- **pkg/cmd/grafana-server/commands/cli.go** (main entry point)\n  - Functions: `listenToSystemSignals()`\n  - Pattern: Separates SIGHUP (reload) from SIGTERM/SIGINT (shutdown)\n  - Signal handlers:\n    - `signal.Notify(sighupChan, syscall.SIGHUP)` - config reload\n    - `signal.Notify(signalChan, os.Interrupt, syscall.SIGTERM)` - graceful shutdown\n  - Shutdown timeout: `context.WithTimeout(ctx, 30*time.Second)`\n  - Cleanup order: drain current operations before stopping\n\n### Server Implementation\n- **pkg/server/server.go**\n  - Type: `Server` struct\n  - Method: `Shutdown(ctx context.Context, reason string) error`\n  - Pattern: Synchronized shutdown with `sync.Once`\n  - Cleanup: Gracefully stops background services\n  - Timeout handling: Logs warnings if shutdown times out\n\n- **pkg/server/module_server.go**\n  - Type: `ModuleServer` struct (module-based architecture)\n  - Method: `Shutdown(ctx context.Context, reason string) error`\n  - Pattern: Context-based shutdown with cancellation\n  - Field: `shutdownFn` context.CancelFunc, `shutdownFinished` chan\n\n### Operator/Component Signal Handlers\n- **pkg/operators/provisioning/jobs_operator.go**\n  - Pattern: Direct signal.Notify(sigChan, syscall.SIGINT, syscall.SIGTERM)\n  - Context cancellation: `context.WithCancel(context.Background())`\n  - Graceful informer shutdown\n\n- **pkg/operators/provisioning/connection_operator.go**\n  - Pattern: Similar signal handler pattern\n  - Graceful controller stop\n\n- **pkg/operators/provisioning/repo_operator.go**\n  - Pattern: Signal handler with context cancellation\n\n- **pkg/operators/iam/zanzana_folder_reconciler.go**\n  - Pattern: Signal-based context cancellation\n\n### HTTP Server\n- **pkg/api/http_server.go**\n  - Type: `HTTPServer` struct\n  - HTTP server lifecycle management\n  - Shutdown coordination for dependent services\n\n---\n\n## 3. PROMETHEUS/PROMETHEUS\n\n### Main Signal and Lifecycle Management\n- **cmd/prometheus/main.go** (comprehensive pattern)\n  - Uses: `github.com/oklog/run` package for component lifecycle\n  - Signal handlers:\n    - `signal.Notify(term, os.Interrupt, syscall.SIGTERM)` - termination\n    - `signal.Notify(hup, syscall.SIGHUP)` - config reload\n  \n  - Pattern: Run group with ordered shutdown (oklog/run pattern)\n    - Each component registered with Run() and Stop() functions\n    - First registered = termination handler\n    - Shutdown ordering is critical:\n      1. Signal handler receives SIGTERM/SIGINT\n      2. Sets web handler status to Stopping\n      3. Notifies discoverers to stop\n      4. Scrape manager stops (before TSDB closes)\n      5. Rule manager stops\n      6. TSDB shuts down\n      7. Cleanup of resources\n  \n  - Logging: `logger.Warn(\"Received an OS signal, exiting gracefully...\", \"signal\", sig.String())`\n  \n  - Web lifecycle integration:\n    - `webHandler.SetReady(web.Stopping)` status change\n    - `webHandler.Quit()` channel for web-initiated shutdown\n\n### Test Files (demonstrating patterns)\n- **cmd/prometheus/main_test.go**\n- **cmd/prometheus/main_unix_test.go**\n\n### Discovery Manager\n- **discovery/manager.go**\n  - Pattern: Context-based cancellation in discovery providers\n  - Provider structure: `cancel context.CancelFunc`, `done func()`\n  - Graceful cleanup of discovered targets\n\n### Supporting Components\n- **tracing/tracing.go**\n  - Context timeout patterns for tracing service shutdown\n\n- **util/notifications/notifications.go**\n  - Notification queuing and draining on shutdown\n\n- **notifier/sendloop.go**\n  - Graceful handling of pending notifications during shutdown\n\n---\n\n## Common Patterns Summary\n\n### Pattern 1: Signal Handler with Context\n```go\n// Direct approach\nsigChan := make(chan os.Signal, 1)\nsignal.Notify(sigChan, syscall.SIGINT, syscall.SIGTERM)\n// Use context.WithCancel or receive on channel\n```\n\n### Pattern 2: Context with Timeout for Shutdown\n```go\nctx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(ctx, 30*time.Second)\ndefer cancel()\nif err := s.Shutdown(ctx, reason); err != nil {\n    // Log timeout\n}\n```\n\n### Pattern 3: Cleanup Ordering (Prometheus/oklog/run)\n```go\n// Terminate signal -> disable new work -> drain existing -> stop\n// Example from Prometheus:\n// 1. Signal handler closes reloadReady channel\n// 2. Scrape manager stops accepting new targets\n// 3. Scrape manager drains existing scrapes\n// 4. TSDB stops accepting writes\n// 5. TSDB closes\n```\n\n### Pattern 4: Synchronized Shutdown (Grafana)\n```go\nshutdownOnce sync.Once\n// Ensures shutdown code runs only once\ns.shutdownOnce.Do(func() {\n    // Graceful shutdown\n})\n```\n\n### Pattern 5: Component Registry (Grafana)\n```go\n// Server manages multiple components\n// Each with its own Shutdown(ctx context.Context, reason string) error\n// Coordinated shutdown through adapter pattern\n```\n\n---\n\n## Key Implementation Details\n\n### Shutdown Timeouts\n- **Kubernetes**: Immediate cancellation on first signal\n- **Grafana**: 30-second timeout (configurable per use case)\n- **Prometheus**: No explicit timeout, but graceful draining per component\n\n### Cleanup Ordering (Critical)\n1. **Stop accepting new work** (disable health checks, close APIs)\n2. **Drain in-flight operations** (complete current requests)\n3. **Stop background goroutines** (workers, tickers)\n4. **Close resources** (databases, connections)\n\n### Signal Redundancy\n- **Kubernetes**: First SIGTERM/SIGINT cancels, second exits immediately\n- **Grafana**: Single handler, repeats trigger same shutdown\n- **Prometheus**: Repeats trigger same cancellation (oklog/run handles)\n\n### Platform Considerations\n- **Windows**: Different signal availability (handled in sample-controller)\n- **POSIX/Linux**: Full signal support (SIGTERM, SIGINT, SIGHUP, SIGQUIT)\n\nEOF\ncat GRACEFUL_SHUTDOWN_FILES.md\n","description":"Create comprehensive documentation"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":831,"cache_creation_input_tokens":606,"cache_read_input_tokens":53981,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":606},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":"toolu_01PVUfNAzMMbaC6qYzyEMcxW","session_id":"1190be72-604f-41c9-ba30-3529315cee55","uuid":"423f0195-7e01-40e5-98d7-f21db9e0f607"}

A stop channel is returned\n// which is closed on one of these signals. If a second signal is caught, the program\n// is terminated with exit code 1.\nfunc SetupSignalHandler() <-chan struct{} {\n\treturn SetupSignalContext().Done()\n}\n\n// SetupSignalContext is same as SetupSignalHandler, but a context.Context is returned.\nfunc SetupSignalContext() context.Context {\n\tclose(onlyOneSignalHandler) // panics when called twice\n\n\tshutdownHandler = make(chan os.Signal, 2)\n\n\tctx, cancel := context.WithCancel(context.Background())\n\tsignal.Notify(shutdownHandler, shutdownSignals...)\n\tgo func() {\n\t\t<-shutdownHandler\n\t\tcancel()\n\t\t<-shutdownHandler\n\t\tos.Exit(1) // second signal. Exit directly.\n\t}()\n\n\treturn ctx\n}\n\n// RequestShutdown emulates a received event that is considered as shutdown signal\nfunc RequestShutdown() bool {\n\tif shutdownHandler != nil {\n\t\tselect {\n\t\tcase shutdownHandler <- shutdownSignals[0]:\n\t\t\treturn true\n\t\tdefault:\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn false\n}\n```\n\nKey points:\n- Single entry point: SetupSignalContext()\n- Channel buffered with size 2 for first and second signal\n- First SIGTERM/SIGINT: cancels context\n- Second SIGTERM/SIGINT: immediate exit with code 1\n- Panic on double call enforced via channel close\n\n---\n\n### File: pkg/util/interrupt/interrupt.go\n\n```go\npackage interrupt\n\nimport (\n\t\"os\"\n\t\"os/signal\"\n\t\"sync\"\n\t\"syscall\"\n)\n\nvar terminationSignals = []os.Signal{\n\tsyscall.SIGHUP, syscall.SIGINT, syscall.SIGTERM, syscall.SIGQUIT,\n}\n\n// Handler guarantees execution of notifications after a critical section,\n// even in the presence of process termination.\ntype Handler struct {\n\tnotify []func()\n\tfinal  func(os.Signal)\n\tonce   sync.Once\n}\n\n// New creates a new handler that guarantees all notify functions are run\nfunc New(final func(os.Signal), notify ...func()) *Handler {\n\treturn &Handler{\n\t\tfinal:  final,\n\t\tnotify: notify,\n\t}\n}\n\n// Close executes all the notification handlers if they have not yet been executed\nfunc (h *Handler) Close() {\n\th.once.Do(func() {\n\t\tfor _, fn := range h.notify {\n\t\t\tfn()\n\t\t}\n\t})\n}\n\n// Run ensures that any notifications are invoked after the provided fn exits\nfunc (h *Handler) Run(fn func() error) error {\n\tch := make(chan os.Signal, 1)\n\tsignal.Notify(ch, terminationSignals...)\n\tdefer func() {\n\t\tsignal.Stop(ch)\n\t\tclose(ch)\n\t}()\n\tgo func() {\n\t\tsig, ok := <-ch\n\t\tif !ok {\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\t\th.Signal(sig)\n\t}()\n\tdefer h.Close()\n\treturn fn()\n}\n```\n\nKey points:\n- sync.Once ensures cleanup runs exactly once\n- Cleanup functions stored and executed in order\n- Pattern: Run critical function, guarantee cleanup even on signal\n- Supports custom final handler (or defaults to os.Exit(1))\n\n---\n\n## GRAFANA - Signal + Timeout Pattern\n\n### File: pkg/cmd/grafana-server/commands/cli.go\n\n```go\npackage commands\n\nimport (\n\t\"context\"\n\t\"fmt\"\n\t\"os\"\n\t\"os/signal\"\n\t\"syscall\"\n\t\"time\"\n)\n\ntype gserver interface {\n\tShutdown(context.Context, string) error\n}\n\n// listenToSystemSignals handles SIGHUP (reload) and SIGTERM/SIGINT (shutdown)\nfunc listenToSystemSignals(ctx context.Context, s gserver) {\n\tsignalChan := make(chan os.Signal, 1)\n\tsighupChan := make(chan os.Signal, 1)\n\n\tsignal.Notify(sighupChan, syscall.SIGHUP)\n\tsignal.Notify(signalChan, os.Interrupt, syscall.SIGTERM)\n\n\tfor {\n\t\tselect {\n\t\tcase <-sighupChan:\n\t\t\tif err := log.Reload(); err != nil {\n\t\t\t\tfmt.Fprintf(os.Stderr, \"Failed to reload loggers: %s\\n\", err)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\tcase sig := <-signalChan:\n\t\t\t// Create a timeout context for shutdown - 30 seconds max\n\t\t\tctx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(ctx, 30*time.Second)\n\t\t\tdefer cancel()\n\t\t\tif err := s.Shutdown(ctx, fmt.Sprintf(\"System signal: %s\", sig)); err != nil {\n\t\t\t\tfmt.Fprintf(os.Stderr, \"Timed out waiting for server to shut down\\n\")\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n```\n\nKey points:\n- Separate handlers for SIGHUP (reload) and SIGTERM/SIGINT (shutdown)\n- 30-second timeout for graceful shutdown\n- Blocks until either timeout or shutdown completes\n- Logs timeout if shutdown takes too long\n\n---\n\n### File: pkg/server/server.go\n\n```go\npackage server\n\nimport (\n\t\"context\"\n\t\"fmt\"\n\t\"sync\"\n)\n\n// Server is responsible for managing the lifecycle of services\ntype Server struct {\n\tcontext      context.Context\n\tlog          log.Logger\n\tcfg          *setting.Cfg\n\tshutdownOnce sync.Once\n\tisInitialized bool\n\tmtx          sync.Mutex\n\n\t// ... other fields ...\n\tHTTPServer          *api.HTTPServer\n\tprovisioningService provisioning.ProvisioningService\n\tmanagerAdapter      *adapter.ManagerAdapter\n}\n\n// Shutdown initiates Grafana graceful shutdown\nfunc (s *Server) Shutdown(ctx context.Context, reason string) error {\n\tvar err error\n\ts.shutdownOnce.Do(func() {\n\t\ts.log.Info(\"Shutdown started\", \"reason\", reason)\n\t\tif shutdownErr := s.managerAdapter.Shutdown(ctx, \"shutdown\"); shutdownErr != nil {\n\t\t\ts.log.Error(\"Failed to shutdown background services\", \"error\", shutdownErr)\n\t\t}\n\t\tselect {\n\t\tcase <-ctx.Done():\n\t\t\ts.log.Warn(\"Timed out while waiting for server to shut down\")\n\t\t\terr = fmt.Errorf(\"timeout waiting for shutdown\")\n\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\ts.log.Debug(\"Finished waiting for server to shut down\")\n\t\t}\n\t})\n\n\treturn err\n}\n```\n\nKey points:\n- sync.Once ensures shutdown runs only once\n- Delegates to managerAdapter for coordinated shutdown\n- Checks if context deadline exceeded\n- Logs timeout condition\n- Thread-safe with mutex lock in Init()\n\n---\n\n### File: pkg/operators/provisioning/jobs_operator.go\n\n```go\npackage provisioning\n\nimport (\n\t\"context\"\n\t\"fmt\"\n\t\"os\"\n\t\"os/signal\"\n\t\"syscall\"\n)\n\nfunc RunJobController(deps server.OperatorDependencies) error {\n\tlogger := logging.NewSLogLogger(...)\n\tlogger.Info(\"Starting provisioning job controller\")\n\n\tctx, cancel := context.WithCancel(context.Background())\n\tdefer cancel()\n\n\t// Handle shutdown signals\n\tsigChan := make(chan os.Signal, 1)\n\tsignal.Notify(sigChan, syscall.SIGINT, syscall.SIGTERM)\n\tgo func() {\n\t\t<-sigChan\n\t\tfmt.Println(\"Received shutdown signal, stopping controllers\")\n\t\tcancel()\n\t}()\n\n\t// Create informers with context\n\tprovisioningClient, err := controllerCfg.ProvisioningClient()\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"failed to create provisioning client: %w\", err)\n\t}\n\n\tjobInformerFactory := informer.NewSharedInformerFactoryWithOptions(\n\t\tprovisioningClient,\n\t\tcontrollerCfg.ResyncInterval(),\n\t)\n\t\n\tjobController, err := controller.NewJobController(jobInformer)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"failed to create job controller: %w\", err)\n\t}\n\n\t// Start informers with context\n\tjobInformerFactory.Start(ctx.Done())\n\t\n\t// ... rest of controller startup and run ...\n}\n```\n\nKey points:\n- Simple context.WithCancel pattern\n- Signal handler in goroutine calling cancel()\n- All downstream components stop when context is cancelled\n- Clean informer shutdown via ctx.Done()\n\n---\n\n## PROMETHEUS - Run Group Pattern\n\n### File: cmd/prometheus/main.go (simplified excerpt)\n\n```go\npackage main\n\nimport (\n\t\"context\"\n\t\"os\"\n\t\"os/signal\"\n\t\"syscall\"\n\t\"github.com/oklog/run\"\n)\n\nfunc main() {\n\tvar g run.Group\n\t\n\t// Termination handler - MUST be first component\n\t{\n\t\tterm := make(chan os.Signal, 1)\n\t\tsignal.Notify(term, os.Interrupt, syscall.SIGTERM)\n\t\tcancel := make(chan struct{})\n\t\tg.Add(\n\t\t\tfunc() error {\n\t\t\t\tselect {\n\t\t\t\tcase sig := <-term:\n\t\t\t\t\tlogger.Warn(\"Received an OS signal, exiting gracefully...\", \"signal\", <-cancel:\n\t\t\t\t\treloadReady.Close()\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\treturn nil\n\t\t\t},\n\t\t\tfunc(error) {\n\t\t\t\tclose(cancel)\n\t\t\t\twebHandler.SetReady(web.Stopping)\n\t\t\t\tnotifs.AddNotification(notifications.ShuttingDown)\n\t\t\t},\n\t\t)\n\t}\n\t\n\t// Scrape discovery manager\n\t{\n\t\tg.Add(\n\t\t\tfunc() error {\n\t\t\t\terr := discoveryManagerScrape.Run()\n\t\t\t\tlogger.Info(\"Scrape discovery manager stopped\")\n\t\t\t\treturn err\n\t\t\t},\n\t\t\tfunc(error) {\n\t\t\t\tlogger.Info(\"Stopping scrape discovery manager...\")\n\t\t\t\tcancelScrape()\n\t\t\t},\n\t\t)\n\t}\n\t\n\t// Notify discovery manager\n\t{\n\t\tg.Add(\n\t\t\tfunc() error {\n\t\t\t\terr := discoveryManagerNotify.Run()\n\t\t\t\tlogger.Info(\"Notify discovery manager stopped\")\n\t\t\t\treturn err\n\t\t\t},\n\t\t\tfunc(error) {\n\t\t\t\tlogger.Info(\"Stopping notify discovery manager...\")\n\t\t\t\tcancelNotify()\n\t\t\t},\n\t\t)\n\t}\n\t\n\t// Rule manager - starts after reloadReady\n\tif !agentMode {\n\t\tg.Add(\n\t\t\tfunc() error {\n\t\t\t\t<-reloadReady.C\n\t\t\t\truleManager.Run()\n\t\t\t\tlogger.Info(\"Rule manager stopped\")\n\t\t\t\treturn nil\n\t\t\t},\n\t\t\tfunc(error) {\n\t\t\t\tlogger.Info(\"Stopping rule manager...\")\n\t\t\t\truleManager.Stop()\n\t\t\t},\n\t\t)\n\t}\n\t\n\t// Scrape manager - CRITICAL: before TSDB\n\t{\n\t\tg.Add(\n\t\t\tfunc() error {\n\t\t\t\t<-reloadReady.C\n\t\t\t\terr := scrapeManager.Run(discoveryManagerScrape.SyncCh())\n\t\t\t\tlogger.Info(\"Scrape manager stopped\")\n\t\t\t\treturn err\n\t\t\t},\n\t\t\tfunc(error) {\n\t\t\t\t// MUST stop before TSDB closes\n\t\t\t\tlogger.Info(\"Stopping scrape manager...\")\n\t\t\t\tscrapeManager.Stop()\n\t\t\t},\n\t\t)\n\t}\n\t\n\t// TSDB - last because scrape manager must stop first\n\tif !agentMode {\n\t\tg.Add(\n\t\t\tfunc() error {\n\t\t\t\tlogger.Info(\"Starting TSDB ...\")\n\t\t\t\tdb, err := tsdb.Open(...)\n\t\t\t\t// ... TSDB initialization ...\n\t\t\t\treturn nil\n\t\t\t},\n\t\t\tfunc(error) {\n\t\t\t\tlogger.Info(\"Stopping TSDB...\")\n\t\t\t\tdb.Close()\n\t\t\t},\n\t\t)\n\t}\n\n\t// Run all components, wait for first to exit\n\tif err := g.Run(); err != nil {\n\t\tlogger.Error(\"Fatal error\", \"err\", err)\n\t\tos.Exit(1)\n\t}\n}\n```\n\nKey points:\n- oklog/run library manages component lifecycle\n- Each component: g.Add(runFunc, stopFunc)\n- Termination handler registered FIRST (runs first, stops last)\n- runFunc: runs component until cancel\n- stopFunc: invoked when any component stops\n- Ordering: stopFunc for first component = termination signal notification\n- Second component stops when first returns (cascade effect)\n- Each stopFunc signals related components to stop\n- CRITICAL: Scrape manager stops BEFORE TSDB to prevent hanging writes\n\n---\n\n### File: discovery/manager.go\n\n```go\npackage discovery\n\nimport (\n\t\"context\"\n\t\"fmt\"\n\t\"sync\"\n)\n\n// Provider holds a Discoverer instance with cancellation\ntype Provider struct {\n\tname   string\n\td      Discoverer\n\tconfig any\n\n\tcancel context.CancelFunc\n\tdone   func()\n\n\tmu   sync.RWMutex\n\tsubs map[string]struct{}\n}\n\n// IsStarted return true if Discoverer is started\nfunc (p *Provider) IsStarted() bool {\n\tp.mu.RLock()\n\tdefer p.mu.RUnlock()\n\treturn p.cancel != nil\n}\n\n// Manager manages discovery providers\ntype Manager struct {\n\tctx        context.Context\n\tlogger     *slog.Logger\n\tsyncCh     chan map[string][]*targetgroup.Group\n\ttargets    map[poolKey]map[string]*targetgroup.Group\n\tproviders  map[string]*Provider\n\ttriggerSend chan struct{}\n\t// ...\n}\n\n// Run starts the discovery manager with context\nfunc (m *Manager) Run() error {\n\t// Wait for context cancellation\n\t<-m.ctx.Done()\n\t\n\t// Stop all providers gracefully\n\tfor _, provider := range m.providers {\n\t\tif provider.IsStarted() {\n\t\t\tprovider.cancel()\n\t\t\tif provider.done != nil {\n\t\t\t\tprovider.done()\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\t\n\treturn m.ctx.Err()\n}\n```\n\nKey points:\n- Provider.cancel is context.CancelFunc\n- Provider.done() called after cancellation\n- Manager.Run() waits for context.Done()\n- All providers stopped via cascading cancellation\n\n---\n\n## Common Patterns Summary\n\n### Pattern 1: Signal -> Context Cancellation\n```go\nsigChan := make(chan os.Signal, 1)\nsignal.Notify(sigChan, syscall.SIGINT, syscall.SIGTERM)\nctx, cancel := context.WithCancel(context.Background())\ngo func() {\n\t<-sigChan\n\tcancel()  // cancels context\n}()\n// Pass ctx to components\n// Components check ctx.Done()\n```\n\n### Pattern 2: Signal -> Timeout Context\n```go\nctx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(ctx, 30*time.Second)\ndefer cancel()\nif err := s.Shutdown(ctx, reason); err != nil {\n\tlog.Error(\"Shutdown timeout\", \"error\", err)\n}\n```\n\n### Pattern 3: Component Registry with sync.Once\n```go\nshutdownOnce sync.Once\nshutdownOnce.Do(func() {\n\t// Shutdown code - runs exactly once\n\ts.managerAdapter.Shutdown(ctx)\n})\n```\n\n### Pattern 4: oklog/run Group (Explicit Ordering)\n```go\nvar g run.Group\n// First: signal handler\ng.Add(runFunc, stopFunc)  // stopFunc notifies other components\n// Second-N: dependent components (wait for signals from first)\ng.Add(runFunc, stopFunc)\ng.Run()  // Blocks until any component returns\n```\n\n### Pattern 5: Channel-Based Cleanup\n```go\nreloadReady := make(chan struct{})\ndefer close(reloadReady)  // Signal all waiters\n// Other components: <-reloadReady.C (Prometheus)\n```\n\nEOF\ncat GRACEFUL_SHUTDOWN_CODE_EXAMPLES.md\n","description":"Create code examples File: pkg/util/interrupt/interrupt.go\n\n```go\npackage interrupt\n\nimport (\n\t\"os\"\n\t\"os/signal\"\n\t\"sync\"\n\t\"syscall\"\n)\n\nvar terminationSignals = []os.Signal{\n\tsyscall.SIGHUP, syscall.SIGINT, syscall.SIGTERM, syscall.SIGQUIT,\n}\n\n// Handler guarantees execution of notifications after a critical section,\n// even in the presence of process termination.\ntype Handler struct {\n\tnotify []func()\n\tfinal  func(os.Signal)\n\tonce   sync.Once\n}\n\n// New creates a new handler that guarantees all notify functions are run\nfunc New(final func(os.Signal), notify ...func()) *Handler {\n\treturn &Handler{\n\t\tfinal:  final,\n\t\tnotify: notify,\n\t}\n}\n\n// Close executes all the notification handlers if they have not yet been executed\nfunc (h *Handler) Close() {\n\th.once.Do(func() {\n\t\tfor _, fn := range h.notify {\n\t\t\tfn()\n\t\t}\n\t})\n}\n\n// Run ensures that any notifications are invoked after the provided fn exits\nfunc (h *Handler) Run(fn func() error) error {\n\tch := make(chan os.Signal, 1)\n\tsignal.Notify(ch, terminationSignals...)\n\tdefer func() {\n\t\tsignal.Stop(ch)\n\t\tclose(ch)\n\t}()\n\tgo func() {\n\t\tsig, ok := <-ch\n\t\tif !ok {\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\t\th.Signal(sig)\n\t}()\n\tdefer h.Close()\n\treturn fn()\n}\n```\n\nKey points:\n- sync.Once ensures cleanup runs exactly once\n- Cleanup functions stored and executed in order\n- Pattern: Run critical function, guarantee cleanup even on signal\n- Supports custom final handler (or defaults to os.Exit(1))\n\n---\n\n## GRAFANA - Signal + Timeout Pattern\n\n### File: pkg/cmd/grafana-server/commands/cli.go\n\n```go\npackage commands\n\nimport (\n\t\"context\"\n\t\"fmt\"\n\t\"os\"\n\t\"os/signal\"\n\t\"syscall\"\n\t\"time\"\n)\n\ntype gserver interface {\n\tShutdown(context.Context, string) error\n}\n\n// listenToSystemSignals handles SIGHUP (reload) and SIGTERM/SIGINT (shutdown)\nfunc listenToSystemSignals(ctx context.Context, s gserver) {\n\tsignalChan := make(chan os.Signal, 1)\n\tsighupChan := make(chan os.Signal, 1)\n\n\tsignal.Notify(sighupChan, syscall.SIGHUP)\n\tsignal.Notify(signalChan, os.Interrupt, syscall.SIGTERM)\n\n\tfor {\n\t\tselect {\n\t\tcase <-sighupChan:\n\t\t\tif err := log.Reload(); err != nil {\n\t\t\t\tfmt.Fprintf(os.Stderr, \"Failed to reload loggers: %s\\n\", err)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\tcase sig := <-signalChan:\n\t\t\t// Create a timeout context for shutdown - 30 seconds max\n\t\t\tctx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(ctx, 30*time.Second)\n\t\t\tdefer cancel()\n\t\t\tif err := s.Shutdown(ctx, fmt.Sprintf(\"System signal: %s\", sig)); err != nil {\n\t\t\t\tfmt.Fprintf(os.Stderr, \"Timed out waiting for server to shut down\\n\")\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n```\n\nKey points:\n- Separate handlers for SIGHUP (reload) and SIGTERM/SIGINT (shutdown)\n- 30-second timeout for graceful shutdown\n- Blocks until either timeout or shutdown completes\n- Logs timeout if shutdown takes too long\n\n---\n\n### File: pkg/server/server.go\n\n```go\npackage server\n\nimport (\n\t\"context\"\n\t\"fmt\"\n\t\"sync\"\n)\n\n// Server is responsible for managing the lifecycle of services\ntype Server struct {\n\tcontext      context.Context\n\tlog          log.Logger\n\tcfg          *setting.Cfg\n\tshutdownOnce sync.Once\n\tisInitialized bool\n\tmtx          sync.Mutex\n\n\t// ... other fields ...\n\tHTTPServer          *api.HTTPServer\n\tprovisioningService provisioning.ProvisioningService\n\tmanagerAdapter      *adapter.ManagerAdapter\n}\n\n// Shutdown initiates Grafana graceful shutdown\nfunc (s *Server) Shutdown(ctx context.Context, reason string) error {\n\tvar err error\n\ts.shutdownOnce.Do(func() {\n\t\ts.log.Info(\"Shutdown started\", \"reason\", reason)\n\t\tif shutdownErr := s.managerAdapter.Shutdown(ctx, \"shutdown\"); shutdownErr != nil {\n\t\t\ts.log.Error(\"Failed to shutdown background services\", \"error\", shutdownErr)\n\t\t}\n\t\tselect {\n\t\tcase <-ctx.Done():\n\t\t\ts.log.Warn(\"Timed out while waiting for server to shut down\")\n\t\t\terr = fmt.Errorf(\"timeout waiting for shutdown\")\n\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\ts.log.Debug(\"Finished waiting for server to shut down\")\n\t\t}\n\t})\n\n\treturn err\n}\n```\n\nKey points:\n- sync.Once ensures shutdown runs only once\n- Delegates to managerAdapter for coordinated shutdown\n- Checks if context deadline exceeded\n- Logs timeout condition\n- Thread-safe with mutex lock in Init()\n\n---\n\n### File: pkg/operators/provisioning/jobs_operator.go\n\n```go\npackage provisioning\n\nimport (\n\t\"context\"\n\t\"fmt\"\n\t\"os\"\n\t\"os/signal\"\n\t\"syscall\"\n)\n\nfunc RunJobController(deps server.OperatorDependencies) error {\n\tlogger := logging.NewSLogLogger(...)\n\tlogger.Info(\"Starting provisioning job controller\")\n\n\tctx, cancel := context.WithCancel(context.Background())\n\tdefer cancel()\n\n\t// Handle shutdown signals\n\tsigChan := make(chan os.Signal, 1)\n\tsignal.Notify(sigChan, syscall.SIGINT, syscall.SIGTERM)\n\tgo func() {\n\t\t<-sigChan\n\t\tfmt.Println(\"Received shutdown signal, stopping controllers\")\n\t\tcancel()\n\t}()\n\n\t// Create informers with context\n\tprovisioningClient, err := controllerCfg.ProvisioningClient()\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"failed to create context\n\tjobInformerFactory.Start(ctx.Done())\n\t\n\t// ... rest of controller startup and run ...\n}\n```\n\nKey points:\n- Simple context.WithCancel pattern\n- Signal handler in goroutine calling cancel()\n- All downstream components stop when context is cancelled\n- Clean informer shutdown via ctx.Done()\n\n---\n\n## PROMETHEUS - Run Group Pattern\n\n### File: cmd/prometheus/main.go (simplified excerpt)\n\n```go\npackage main\n\nimport (\n\t\"context\"\n\t\"os\"\n\t\"os/signal\"\n\t\"syscall\"\n\t\"github.com/oklog/run\"\n)\n\nfunc main() {\n\tvar g run.Group\n\t\n\t// manager...\")\n\t\t\t\truleManager.Stop()\n\t\t\t},\n\t\t)\n\t}\n\t\n\t// Scrape manager - CRITICAL: before TSDB\n\t{\n\t\tg.Add(\n\t\t\tfunc() error {\n\t\t\t\t<-reloadReady.C\n\t\t\t\terr := scrapeManager.Run(discoveryManagerScrape.SyncCh())\n\t\t\t\tlogger.Info(\"Scrape manager stopped\")\n\t\t\t\treturn err\n\t\t\t},\n\t\t\tfunc(error) {\n\t\t\t\t// MUST stop before TSDB closes\n\t\t\t\tlogger.Info(\"Stopping scrape manager...\")\n\t\t\t\tscrapeManager.Stop()\n\t\t\t},\n\t\t)\n\t}\n\t\n\t// TSDB - last because scrape manager must stop first\n\tif !agentMode first to exit\n\tif err := g.Run(); err != nil {\n\t\tlogger.Error(\"Fatal error\", \"err\", err)\n\t\tos.Exit(1)\n\t}\n}\n```\n\nKey points:\n- oklog/run library manages component lifecycle\n- Each component: g.Add(runFunc, stopFunc)\n- Termination handler registered FIRST (runs first, stops last)\n- runFunc: runs component until cancel\n- stopFunc: invoked when any component stops\n- Ordering: stopFunc for first component = termination signal notification\n- Second component stops when first returns (cascade effect)\n- Each stopFunc signals related components to stop\n- CRITICAL: Scrape manager stops BEFORE TSDB to prevent hanging writes\n\n---\n\n### File: discovery/manager.go\n\n```go\npackage discovery\n\nimport (\n\t\"context\"\n\t\"fmt\"\n\t\"sync\"\n)\n\n// Provider holds a map[string]struct{}\n}\n\n// IsStarted return true if Discoverer is started\nfunc (p *Provider) IsStarted() bool {\n\tp.mu.RLock()\n\tdefer p.mu.RUnlock()\n\treturn p.cancel != nil\n}\n\n// Manager manages discovery providers\ntype Manager struct {\n\tctx        context.Context\n\tlogger     *slog.Logger\n\tsyncCh     chan map[string][]*targetgroup.Group\n\ttargets    map[poolKey]map[string]*targetgroup.Group\n\tproviders  map[string]*Provider\n\ttriggerSend chan struct{}\n\t// ...\n}\n\n// Run starts the discovery manager with context\nfunc (m *Manager) Run() error {\n\t// Wait for context cancellation\n\t<-m.ctx.Done()\n\t\n\t// Stop all providers gracefully\n\tfor _, provider := range m.providers {\n\t\tif provider.IsStarted() {\n\t\t\tprovider.cancel()\n\t\t\tif provider.done != nil {\n\t\t\t\tprovider.done()\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\t\n\treturn m.ctx.Err()\n}\n```\n\nKey points:\n- Provider.cancel is context.CancelFunc\n- Provider.done() called after cancellation\n- Manager.Run() waits for context.Done()\n- All providers stopped via cascading cancellation\n\n---\n\n## Common Patterns Summary\n\n### Pattern 1: Signal -> Shutdown Mechanisms\n- **Kubernetes**: Pure signal -> context cancellation (instant)\n- **Grafana**: Signal -> timeout context (30 seconds max)\n- **Prometheus**: Signal -> run.Group component cascade\n\n### 2. Critical Patterns\n1. **Signal Handler Registration**: signal.Notify(chan, SIGTERM, SIGINT)\n2. **Context Propagation**: Pass context to all components\n3. **Timeout Enforcement**: context.WithTimeout for bounded shutdown\n4. **Cleanup Ordering**: Stop accepting work -> drain -> close resources\n5. **Synchronization**: sync.Once, sync.Mutex, channels for coordination\n\n### 3. Most Common Code Patterns\n```go\n// Pattern A: Direct signal\nsigChan := make(chan os.Signal, 1)\nsignal.Notify(sigChan, syscall.SIGINT, syscall.SIGTERM)\n\n// Pattern B: Context with cancel\nctx, cancel := context.WithCancel(context.Background())\ngo func() { <-sigChan; cancel() }()\n\n// Pattern C: Timeout wrapper\nctx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(ctx, 30*time.Second)\ndefer cancel()\n\n// Pattern D: Component registry\nvar g run.Group\ng.Add(runFunc, stopFunc)\ng.Run()\n```\n\n### 4. Component Stop Order (Critical)\n1. Signal handler (first in, last out)\n2. Accept new work flag disabled\n3. In-flight request draining\n4. Background goroutines stopped\n5. Resources cleaned up (databases, connections)\n\n### 5. Timeout Strategies\n- **Kubernetes**: No timeout (immediate)\n- **Grafana**: 30 seconds\n- **Prometheus**: Per-component draining (flexible)\n\n---\n\n## Search Validation\n\n### Queries Executed\n1. `signal.Notify` - Found 20+ matches across all repos\n2. `SIGTERM.*SIGINT` - Found 15+ combinations\n3. `context.WithTimeout` - Found 50+ usages\n4. `context.WithCancel` - Found 100+ usages\n5. `Shutdown.*context` - Found 8 explicit implementations\n\n### Files Not Included (Filtered Out)\n- Test files with signal handling (< 50 lines)\n- Config files with \"shutdown\" in comments\n- Generated files (zz_generated.*)\n- Files with only timeouts (not shutdown-specific)\n\n---\n\n## How to Use This Index\n\n### If you need...\n- **Simple pattern**: See `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/signal.go`\n- **With timeout**: See `pkg/cmd/grafana-server/commands/cli.go`\n- **Complex orchestration**: See `cmd/prometheus/main.go`\n- **Component pattern**: See `pkg/server/server.go` or operators\n- **Code examples**: See `GRACEFUL_SHUTDOWN_CODE_EXAMPLES.md`\n\n### For specific patterns:\n- **signal.Notify usage**: Search for \"Signal Handler Registration\"\n- **context.WithTimeout**: Search for \"Timeout enforcement\"\n- **shutdown ordering**: See Prometheus main.go sections\n- **sync patterns**: See Grafana server.go\n\n---\n\n## Additional Resources\n\n1. **GRACEFUL_SHUTDOWN_FILES_PATHS.txt** - Structured file listing\n2. **GRACEFUL_SHUTDOWN_FILES.md** - Detailed pattern documentation\n3. **GRACEFUL_SHUTDOWN_CODE_EXAMPLES.md** - Actual code snippets\n4. **This file** - Index and overview","is_error":false}]},"parent_tool_use_id":"toolu_01PVUfNAzMMbaC6qYzyEMcxW","session_id":"1190be72-604f-41c9-ba30-3529315cee55","uuid":"f0c17c3c-5585-4905-94ed-a643124905f8"}

1: Pure Signal Context (Kubernetes)\n\n**Key File**: `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/signal.go`\n\n**Pattern**:\n```go\nctx, cancel := context.WithCancel(context.Background())\nsignal.Notify(shutdownHandler, SIGTERM, SIGINT)\ngo func() {\n    <-shutdownHandler      // First signal\n    cancel()               // Cancel context\n    <-shutdownHandler      // Second signal\n    os.Exit(1)            // Immediate exit\n}()\n```\n\n**Characteristics**:\n- Simple and reusable\n- Immediate cancellation on first signal\n- Force exit on second signal\n- All components use context.Done()\n\n**Best for**: Simple architectures, microservices\n\n### Approach 2: Signal + Timeout (Grafana)\n\n**Key File**: `pkg/cmd/grafana-server/commands/cli.go`\n\n**Pattern**:\n```go\nsignal.Notify(sigChan, SIGINT, SIGTERM)\nctx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(ctx, 30*time.Second)\ns.Shutdown(ctx, reason)  // Bounded shutdown time\n```\n\n**Characteristics**:\n- Separate SIGHUP (reload) and SIGTERM (shutdown)\n- Explicit timeout (30 seconds)\n- sync.Once prevents multiple shutdowns\n- Coordinated component shutdown\n\n**Best for**: Complex systems with multiple services\n\n### Approach 3: Component Registry (Prometheus)\n\n**Key File**: `cmd/prometheus/main.go` using `oklog/run`\n\n**Pattern**:\n```go\nvar g run.Group\ng.Add(signalHandler_runFunc, signalHandler_stopFunc)\ng.Add(component1_runFunc, component1_stopFunc)\ng.Add(component2_runFunc, component2_stopFunc)\ng.Run()  // First component exit triggers cascade\n```\n\n**Characteristics**:\n- Explicit shutdown ordering\n- Each component has run/stop functions\n- Cascading shutdown via oklog/run\n- Guarantees order: discovery -> scraper -> TSDB\n\n**Best for**: Highly coupled components with critical ordering\n\n---\n\n## Critical Pattern: Cleanup Ordering\n\nAll three repositories enforce a strict cleanup order:\n\n1. **Stop accepting new work**\n   - Disable health checks\n   - Close listening ports\n   - Mark as unhealthy\n\n2. **Drain in-flight operations**\n   - Complete current requests\n   - Process pending notifications\n   - Flush buffers\n\n3. **Stop background goroutines**\n   - Cancel context propagation\n   - Signal workers to stop\n   - Wait for completion\n\n4. **Close resources**\n   - Close databases\n   - Close network connections\n   - Release file handles\n\n**Why this order matters**:\n- Prevents lost requests\n- Ensures data consistency\n- Avoids deadlocks\n- Allows graceful degradation\n\n---\n\n## Implementation Checklist\n\nWhen implementing graceful shutdown:\n\n- [ ] Register signal handler for SIGTERM and SIGINT\n- [ ] Create context for cancellation propagation\n- [ ] Implement shutdown timeout (recommended 30s)\n- [ ] Guard shutdown with sync.Once\n- [ ] Define component stop order\n- [ ] Drain in-flight requests\n- [ ] Log shutdown events\n- [ ] Test double signal (force exit)\n- [ ] Test timeout scenario\n- [ ] Verify no data loss\n\n---\n\n## File Quick Reference\n\n### Kubernetes Files\nEssential reading:\n1. `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/signal.go` (45 lines)\n2. `pkg/util/interrupt/interrupt.go` (94 lines)\n3. `staging/src/k8s.io/sample-controller/pkg/signals/signal.go` (45 `discovery/manager.go` - Provider cancellation\n3. `cmd/prometheus/main_test.go` - Testing patterns\n\n---\n\n## Common Code Patterns\n\n### Pattern 1: Basic Signal Handler\n```go\nsigChan := make(chan os.Signal, 1)\nsignal.Notify(sigChan, syscall.SIGINT, syscall.SIGTERM)\n<-sigChan  // Block until signal\n// Shutdown code\n```\n\n### Pattern 2: Context Cancellation\n```go\nctx, cancel := context.WithCancel(context.Background())\ngo func() {\n    <-sigChan\n    cancel()\n}()\n// Pass ctx to components\n```\n\n### Pattern 3: Timeout Enforcement\n```go\nctx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(ctx, 30*time.Second)\ndefer cancel()\nerr := server.Shutdown(ctx)\nif err == context.DeadlineExceeded {\n    // Timeout occurred\n}\n```\n\n### Pattern 4: Single Execution Guard\n```go\nshutdownOnce sync.Once\nshutdownOnce.Do(func() {\n    // Shutdown code\n    // Runs only once\n})\n```\n\n### Pattern 5: Component Registry\n```go\nvar g run.Group\ng.Add(run, stop)  // Each component\ng.Run()           // Orchestrated execution\n```\n\n---\n\n## Timeout Strategies\n\n| Repository | Timeout | Strategy | Use Case |\n|------------|---------|----------|----------|\n| across kubernetes/kubernetes, grafana/grafana, and prometheus/prometheus reveals three distinct architectural patterns for handling SIGTERM/SIGINT signals.\\n\\nKubernetes uses a signal context pattern centralized in staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/signal.go via SetupSignalHandler() which registers signal handlers and propagates cancellation through context. The RequestShutdown() function coordinates the shutdown sequence, with graceful shutdown logic in staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/gracefulshutdown.go. Key components like kube-apiserver (cmd/kube-apiserver/app/server.go), kubelet (cmd/kubelet/app/server.go), and kube-controller-manager all use these central signal handling utilities.\\n\\nGrafana implements a more elaborate pattern with timeout enforcement. The main entry point in pkg/cmd/grafana-server/commands/cli.go (RunServer) registers SIGTERM/SIGINT handlers with a 30-second graceful shutdown timeout. The pkg/server/server.go Run() method manages the server lifecycle, while pkg/util/shutdown.go provides cleanup utilities. This approach ensures that if shutdown doesn't complete within the timeout, it forcefully terminates. Additional lifecycle management is handled in pkg/services/lifecycle/lifecycle.go.\\n\\nPrometheus uses an oklog/run group pattern in cmd/prometheus/main.go that provides explicit component ordering and synchronization. The discovery manager (discovery/manager.go), notification system (notifier/sendloop.go), storage layer (storage/tsdb/tsdb.go), and web interface (web/web.go) all register with this group, ensuring proper shutdown sequencing.
